======================================================================
ENDOCRINOLOGY CONSULTATION — SYMPTOM EVALUATION
Record #00001
======================================================================

PATIENT INFORMATION:
  A 40-year-old male patient presented for diabetes risk
  evaluation at the outpatient endocrinology clinic.

PRESENTING COMPLAINTS AND SYMPTOM REVIEW:
  He reports the following symptoms:
    - excessive thirst (polydipsia)
    - generalized weakness and fatigue
    - persistent itching of the skin
    - delayed wound healing
    - muscle stiffness and joint pain
    - hair loss (alopecia)
    - clinical obesity

  He denies:
    - excessive urination (polyuria)
    - sudden unexplained weight loss
    - excessive hunger (polyphagia)
    - recurrent genital thrush infections
    - episodes of visual blurring
    - notable irritability and mood changes
    - partial paresis of the extremities

  Total symptoms reported: 7 out of 14 screened.

CLINICAL ASSESSMENT:
  Based on the symptom profile and clinical evaluation, the patient's
  diabetes risk classification is determined as follows:

  Risk Classification: Positive
  POSITIVE — Patient meets criteria for early-stage diabetes risk. Further laboratory workup including fasting blood glucose and HbA1c is strongly recommended.

--- END OF RECORD #00001 ---

Record #00099
======================================================================

PATIENT INFORMATION:
  A 35-year-old female patient presented for diabetes risk
  evaluation at the outpatient endocrinology clinic.

PRESENTING COMPLAINTS AND SYMPTOM REVIEW:
  She reports the following symptoms:
    - excessive urination (polyuria)
    - excessive thirst (polydipsia)
    - episodes of visual blurring
    - hair loss (alopecia)

  She denies:
    - sudden unexplained weight loss
    - generalized weakness and fatigue
    - excessive hunger (polyphagia)
    - recurrent genital thrush infections
    - persistent itching of the skin
    - notable irritability and mood changes
    - delayed wound healing
    - partial paresis of the extremities
    - muscle stiffness and joint pain
    - clinical obesity

  Total symptoms reported: 4 out of 14 screened.

CLINICAL ASSESSMENT:
  Based on the symptom profile and clinical evaluation, the patient's
  diabetes risk classification is determined as follows:

  Risk Classification: Positive
  POSITIVE — Patient meets criteria for early-stage diabetes risk. Further laboratory workup including fasting blood glucose and HbA1c is strongly recommended.

  POSITIVE — Patient meets criteria for early-stage diabetes risk. Further laboratory workup including fasting blood glucose and HbA1c is strongly recommended.

  A 61-year-old female patient presented for diabetes risk
  evaluation at the outpatient endocrinology clinic.

PRESENTING COMPLAINTS AND SYMPTOM REVIEW:
  She reports the following symptoms:
    - excessive urination (polyuria)
    - excessive hunger (polyphagia)
    - notable irritability and mood changes
    - hair loss (alopecia)

  She denies:
    - excessive thirst (polydipsia)
    - sudden unexplained weight loss
    - generalized weakness and fatigue
    - recurrent genital thrush infections
    - episodes of visual blurring
    - persistent itching of the skin
    - delayed wound healing
    - partial paresis of the extremities
    - muscle stiffness and joint pain
    - clinical obesity

  Total symptoms reported: 4 out of 14 screened.

CLINICAL ASSESSMENT:
  Based on the symptom profile and clinical evaluation, the patient's
  diabetes risk classification is determined as follows:

  Risk Classification: Positive
  POSITIVE — Patient meets criteria for early-stage diabetes risk. Further laboratory workup including fasting blood glucose and HbA1c is strongly recommended.

--- END OF RECORD #00345 ---

    - excessive urination (polyuria)
    - excessive thirst (polydipsia)
    - sudden unexplained weight loss
    - generalized weakness and fatigue
    - excessive hunger (polyphagia)
    - episodes of visual blurring
    - partial paresis of the extremities
    - muscle stiffness and joint pain
    - clinical obesity

  She denies:
    - recurrent genital thrush infections
    - persistent itching of the skin
    - notable irritability and mood changes
    - delayed wound healing
    - hair loss (alopecia)

  Total symptoms reported: 9 out of 14 screened.

CLINICAL ASSESSMENT:
  Based on the symptom profile and clinical evaluation, the patient's
  diabetes risk classification is determined as follows:

  Risk Classification: Positive
  POSITIVE — Patient meets criteria for early-stage diabetes risk. Further laboratory workup including fasting blood glucose and HbA1c is strongly recommended.

  He reports the following symptoms:
    - generalized weakness and fatigue
    - excessive hunger (polyphagia)
    - episodes of visual blurring
    - persistent itching of the skin
    - notable irritability and mood changes
    - delayed wound healing
    - muscle stiffness and joint pain
    - hair loss (alopecia)

  He denies:
    - excessive urination (polyuria)
    - excessive thirst (polydipsia)
    - sudden unexplained weight loss
    - recurrent genital thrush infections
    - partial paresis of the extremities
    - clinical obesity

  Total symptoms reported: 8 out of 14 screened.

CLINICAL ASSESSMENT:
  Based on the symptom profile and clinical evaluation, the patient's
  diabetes risk classification is determined as follows:

  Risk Classification: Negative
  NEGATIVE — Patient does not currently meet criteria for diabetes risk based on symptom screening. Routine follow-up advised.

ENDOCRINOLOGY CONSULTATION — SYMPTOM EVALUATION
Record #00518
======================================================================

PATIENT INFORMATION:
  A 58-year-old female patient presented for diabetes risk
  evaluation at the outpatient endocrinology clinic.

PRESENTING COMPLAINTS AND SYMPTOM REVIEW:
  She reports the following symptoms:
    - excessive urination (polyuria)
    - excessive thirst (polydipsia)
    - sudden unexplained weight loss
    - generalized weakness and fatigue
    - excessive hunger (polyphagia)
    - episodes of visual blurring
    - partial paresis of the extremities
    - muscle stiffness and joint pain
    - clinical obesity

  She denies:
    - recurrent genital thrush infections
    - persistent itching of the skin
    - notable irritability and mood changes
    - delayed wound healing
    - hair loss (alopecia)

  Total symptoms reported: 9 out of 14 screened.

CLINICAL ASSESSMENT:
  Based on the symptom profile and clinical evaluation, the patient's
  diabetes risk classification is determined as follows:

  Risk Classification: Positive
  POSITIVE — Patient meets criteria for early-stage diabetes risk. Further laboratory workup including fasting blood glucose and HbA1c is strongly recommended.
